<span class="updated-on">
<span class="meta-label">Last Updated:</span><time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2026-02-01T03:30:13+00:00" itemprop="dateModified">February 1, 2026</time>					</span></div></header><div class="entry-content single-content"><div class="sassa-form-container" style="background:#fff; color:#000; padding:20px; border-radius:10px; border:2px solid #ccc; max-width:700px; margin:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif;"><h2 style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:20px;" id="sassa-status-check" class="joli-heading jtoc-heading">SASSA Status Check</h2><div class="form-group" style="margin-bottom:15px;">
<label for="id-number">ID Number</label>
<input type="text" id="id-number" placeholder="Enter ID Number" style="width:100%; padding:10px; font-size:16px; border-radius:5px; border:1px solid #ccc;"></div><div class="form-group" style="margin-bottom:15px;">

<input type="text" id="mobile-number" placeholder="Enter Mobile Number" style="width:100%; padding:10px; font-size:16px; border-radius:5px; border:1px solid #ccc;"></div><div style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:15px;">
<button type="button" id="sassa-check-btn" style="padding:10px 20px; font-size:16px; border-radius:5px; border:none; background:#f2a900; color:#fff; cursor:pointer;">Check Status</button></div><div id="sassa-loader" style="display:none; text-align:center; margin-bottom:15px;">Loading…</div><div id="sassa-status-result"></div></div><div class="sassa-update-wrap"><div class="sassa-last-updated" aria-label="Last updated Sassa status date">
Last Updated Sassa Status on : <strong><span id="sassaDate">Loading…</span></strong></div></div><p>Check the status of your SASSA Social Relief of Distress SRD R370 grant online to ensure you receive your payment for the current month. <strong>SASSA Status Check</strong> is important for all applicants to stay informed about the grant updates every 30 days.</p><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-check-sassa-status-srd-status-check-online">SASSA Status Check SRD</h2><ol class="wp-block-list"><li id="htoc-to-sassa-status-check-you-need-to-enter-your-south-african-id-in-the-selected-id-number-section1">To SASSA Status Check you need to enter your South African ID in the selected “ID Number” section on <strong>https://srd.sassa.gov.za</strong>.</li><li id="htoc-enter-your-cell-phone-number-in-the-selected-phone-number-section-that-is-used-to-submit-your-grant-application1">Enter your cell phone number in the selected “Phone Number” section that is used to submit your grant application.</li><li id="htoc-click-on-check-now-button-to-send-your-request-to-sassacheck-database1">Click on ‘Check Now‘ button to send your request to <strong>SASSA database</strong>.</li><li id="htoc-sassa-status-check-system-will-display-the-month-for-which-your-grant-has-been-approved-and-display-it-with-your-application-id-reference-number1"><strong>SASSA Status Check</strong> system will display the month for which your grant has been approved and display it with your Application ID (Reference number).</li></ol><p>With online status you will find your grant collection dates for the current month and stay updated on your R350 and social relief grant application eligibility. You can view the Status Check result below.</p><div id="wpj-jtoc" class="wpj-jtoc wpj-jtoc--main --jtoc-the-content --jtoc-theme-original --jtoc-title-align-center --jtoc-toggle-icon --jtoc-toggle-position-right --jtoc-toggle-1 --jtoc-header-as-toggle --jtoc-headings-full-row-clickable --jtoc-has-custom-styles --jtoc-is-folded --jtoc-animate" ><div class="wpj-jtoc--toc " ><div class="wpj-jtoc--header"><div class="wpj-jtoc--header-main"><div class="wpj-jtoc--title --has-icon"><div class="title-icon">

This course ensures the smooth and conflict-free allotment of funds to intended beneficiaries.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-track-sassa-srd-r350-grant-application-status-through-whatsapp-messaging">SRD Status Check for R350 on WhatsApp</h3><p>The official <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/what-is-sassa-whatsapp-number/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA WhatsApp Number</a></strong> provides SRD status for R350 applicants. Then you will receive a prompt with options for status review. We assure you that the government will continue implementing the social relief of distress grant.</p></blockquote><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-checking-the-approval-status-of-your-r350-social-relief-of-distress-grant-application">Check SASSA R350 Grant Status on Phone Call</h3><p>To check if your R350 Social Relief of Distress grant application has been approved, you can verify through <strong>SRD status check</strong> on your phone. cell phone number to receive an OTP.</li><li id="htoc-finally-receive-your-application-status1">Finally, receive your Application Status.</li></ol><p>You will also receive an SMS containing your SASSA application status details, allowing you to collect your grant from any acceptable money collection option you have selected for withdrawal.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center The status report will include the payout amount, along with a Reference ID and App ID.<br>2. <strong>Not Qualified / Rejected</strong>: Unfortunately, your application did not meet the qualification criteria or was declined based on the eligibility requirements.<br><strong>3. Pending</strong>: Your social relief grant is currently pending and will be reviewed by national authorities soon. It could also mean you have not selected a means to access your money, and you need to change the Sassa Payment Method.<br>4. Canceled / Declined: Your grant has been declined for a reason.<br>1. Your monthly income exceeds the minimum threshold.<br>2. Sassa review found an alternative income source in the means test.<br>3. There is more than R624 amount in your bank account or Sassa Gold card.<br>4. Your Identity Information registered in NSFAS and UIF database records.<br>5. <strong>Bank Details Pending</strong>: You have not linked your bank account with Sassa, and it is advised to update your SASSA bank details.</p></div></div></div></div></div><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-sassa-status-check-online-video-guide">Video Guide for How to Check SASSA Status</h3><p>You can check SASSA status online with our step-by-step video guide. <iframe data-lazyloaded="1" src="about:blank" loading="lazy" title="SASSA Status Check Online for SRD R370  January 2026 Payment Dates" width="720" height="405" data-litespeed-src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/IUPpoEaPgbI?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin" allowfullscreen></iframe></div></figure><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-often-is-the-sassa-status-updated">How Often SASSA Status Update</h3><p>The South African Social Security Agency (SASSA) offers monthly status updates concerning the payment status of grants and the status of recipient applications. These updates are usually provided before the predetermined payday schedule established for annual pay dates when funds are to be deposited into beneficiaries’ bank accounts or SASSA cards, facilitating their collection.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-why-is-my-sassa-r350-grant-still-pending-transactions">R350 Grant Status Pending</h3><p>If your R350 grant status is pending it means there is missing banking information to collect your grant. This happens when your payment method is not selected or incorrect information is provided in your application or reapplication.</p><p>Initially, your SASSA status shows as pending when your grant application is in the SASSA review process, which takes about three months from the date of submission. To avoid this inconvenience, please ensure that you provide accurate bank details to receive your grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-change-sassa-bank-details1"><a href="https://sassacheck.com/change-banking-details-sassa/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA Change Bank Details for SRD R350</a></h3><p>If you are a permanent SASSA beneficiary, you have the flexibility to update your bank details for worry-free grant collection. Follow this step-by-step guide on <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/change-banking-details-sassa/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA Change Bank Details</a></strong> for SRD R350. By doing so, you can ensure that you have selected the correct payment method to receive your payouts on time. This way, you can receive cardless payments, providing you with convenient choices for managing your funds.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-sassa-reconsideration-status-check-application1">Check SASSA Reconsideration Status</h3><p>If your SASSA grant application has been rejected, and you have taken the step of submitting an SASSA Reapplication and requesting reconsideration through the <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/sassa-reapplication/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA Reapplication</a></strong> portal, you can easily track the progress of your reapplication. By entering the necessary information and clicking the ‘Send Pin’ button you will receive a One-Time Password (OTP) to confirm your status as the original applicant. Subsequently, your reconsideration status will be promptly displayed within the same section for your convenience.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-delayed-unsuccessful-sassa-r350-grant-payment-what-to-do">SASSA Payment Not Received</h3><p>If you haven’t received your SASSA R350 grant payment yet, there could be several reasons for the delay. If you are already a recipient, the delay might be due to processing time, verification checks, or weekends and public holidays.</p><p>To address the issue, first ensure your payment method is selected and your contact information is accurate. If you find mistake’s proceed to Change SASSA Phone Number to correct your contact details, and similar like update your banking details to ensure your application is up-to-date. Then, please be patient and consider reaching out to PostBank for technical issues if you’re unable to collect your grant money.</p><p>For existing SASSA beneficiaries who haven’t received their payment, it’s best to reach out to SASSA directly. Verify your SASSA status to know whether your grant is active or canceled. You can get immediate assistance regarding the issue by dialing the national authorities’ toll-free cell call center number 0800 60 10 11.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-what-is-the-procedure-for-checking-the-status-of-my-sassa-r350-grant-appeal1">R350 Application Appeal Status</h3><p>If your application for the SRD grant has been rejected, and you’ve taken the necessary steps by successfully submitting your <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/how-to-sassa-appeal-online/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA Appeal</a></strong> application through the DSD (Department of Social Development) on the Independent Tribunal for Social Assistance Appeals (ITSAA) website, and you now wish to verify the status of your R350 appeal for approval, please follow the steps below.</p><ol class="wp-block-list"><li id="htoc-to-check-your-srd-r350-appeal-status-visit-sassacheck-com1">To check your SRD R350 appeal status visit sassacheck.com</li><li id="htoc-log-in-to-the-account-used-to-apply-for-sassa-r350-application1">Log in to the account used to <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/apply-for-sassa-r350/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Apply for Sassa R350</a></strong> application.</li><li id="htoc-select-r350-appeal-status-from-the-application-status-section1">Select “R350 Appeal Status” from the ‘Application Status’ section.</li><li id="htoc-enter-your-id-number-and-application-reference-number1">Enter your ID number and Application Reference Number.</li><li id="htoc-click-submit-to-view-the-current-status-of-your-r350-appeal1">Click ‘submit’ to view the current status of your R350 appeal.</li></ol><p>Following these steps, your status will be displayed, and you will receive a notification with details. If there are any changes needed in your contact information, you can click on the provided link to <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/how-to-update-sassa-grant-application/">update Sassa grant application</a></strong>. This step helps your appeal to be successful, and you will receive an SMS to be able to collect your money.</p><blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow"><p id="htoc-please-note-that-if-you-disagree-with-sassa-s-decision-for-multiple-months-you-ll-need-to-lodge-a-separate-appeal-application-for-each-month-remember-that-you-have-a-window-of-30-to-90-days-to-appeal-so-it-s-essential-to-act-promptly-your-voice-matters-and-the-appeal-process-is-designed-to-ensure-fairness-and-justice1"><strong>Please Note</strong> that if you disagree with SASSA decision for multiple months, you’ll need to lodge a separate appeal application for each month. Remember that you have a window of 30 to 90 days to appeal, so it’s essential to act timely.</p></blockquote><h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-my-sassa-status-is-approved-but-no-sms-received">SASSA Status Approved But No SMS Received</h3><p>The reason for this issue is incorrect contact details, a typo in your application information, limited funds, phone network signal issues, or a system failure. This is a concerning situation when your Sassa Status approved without an SMS because it will prevent you from receiving your payments from the Post Office, Pick n Pay, and retail stores. To fix this follow these steps.</p><ol class="wp-block-list"><li id="htoc-wait-a-few-days-for-potential-sms-delays1">Wait a few days for potential SMS delays.</li><li id="htoc-contact-your-bank-for-system-or-account-issues1">Contact your bank for system or account issues.</li><li id="htoc-verify-your-phone-details-in-sassa-records1">Verify your phone details in SASSA records.</li><li id="htoc-if-no-sms-after-several-days-call-sassa-helpline-0800-601-0111">If no SMS after several days, call SASSA helpline (0800 601 011).</li><li id="htoc-1">You can find SASSA regional office contact numbers on the <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/contact-us/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Contact Us</a></strong> page.</li><li id="htoc-visit-the-nearest-sassa-office-for-direct-support-if-the-issue-persists-and-your-bank-confirms-no-payment-received1">Visit the nearest SASSA office for direct support if the issue persists and your bank confirms no payment received.</li></ol><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-what-srd-grant-is-now-active-status-means">SRD Grant is Active Now Signify Approved</h4><p>When your status displays SRD Grant Is Now Active it signifies that your application for the Social Grant or SRD Social Relief of Distress R350 has been accepted. You will start receiving Sassa money on a monthly basis at scheduled paydays starting from the next month.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-check-if-sassa-approved-your-grant-application">Check if SASSA Approved Your Grant Application</h4><p>You can verify your status online to check if your application has been approved. Here is how to confirm your Social Relief of Distress R350 grant status.</p><ol class="wp-block-list"><li id="htoc-visit-the-sassa-status-check-website-at-https-sassacheck-com1">Visit the SASSA status check website at https://sassacheck.com/</li><li id="htoc-enter-your-south-african-id-and-your-registered-mobile-number1">Enter your South African ID and your Registered Mobile Number.</li><li id="htoc-click-the-check-status-button-to-submit-your-request1">Click the Check Status button to submit your request.</li><li id="htoc-your-r350-status-will-appear-on-the-screen1">Your R350 status will appear on the screen.</li></ol><p>The national agency service also sends you an SMS notification with the payday of the granted month to the registered applicant’s phone number.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-collect-sassa-srd-payments1">How to Collect SASSA SRD Payments</h4><p>Through the SASSA Status Check online service, you will receive an SMS notification indicating the approved payment month. This SMS is crucial to confirm whether your relief funds have been approved for the period, enabling you to collect your grant through your selected payment method.</p><p>To receive your SASSA grant in your bank account, you can update your bank details and effortlessly receive your grant money every month, eliminating the need to visit the SAPO post office or retail shops. For those without a bank account, options include Pick n Pay, Boxer store, Cash Send, or the Post Office.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-why-sassa-status-failed">Why SASSA Status Failed</h4><p>Your SASSA status check fails if your identity verification has failed. This occurs when your personal information mismatches the data with the Department of Home Affairs (DHA). To resolve this issue, you will need to correct the mistakes in your application by updating your SASSA online application.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-why-does-my-sassa-status-result-say-declined">Why SASSA Status Declined</h4><p>The <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/sassa-status-check-declined/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA Status Check Declined</a></strong> for a specific month grant or declined application due to the SASSA review process and the Means Test. Both existing beneficiaries and new applicants can encounter this status if they do not meet the requirements of the Means Test. This assessment evaluates income thresholds and changes in circumstances, such as an increase in your bank balance exceeding R624.</p><p>If you receive a decline notification, you can review the reasons for clarification and take steps to fix your SASSA Declined Grant application.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li id="htoc-your-income-and-assets-threshold-exceed-the-minimum-of-r6241">Your income and assets threshold exceeds the minimum of R624.</li><li id="htoc-your-id-is-registered-for-uif-nsfas-or-sars-benefits1">Your ID is registered for UIF, NSFAS, or SARS benefits.</li><li id="htoc-your-unemployment-status-has-changed1">Your unemployment status has changed.</li><li id="htoc-an-alternative-income-source-is-identified-in-the-sassa-means-test1">An alternative income source is identified in the SASSA Means Test.</li><li id="htoc-your-age-does-not-meet-the-criteria-for-the-applied-grant1">Your age does not meet the criteria for the applied grant.</li></ul><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-collect-sassa-srd-payments">How to Collect SASSA SRD Payments</h4><p>To ensure the receipt of SASSA SRD payments, every applicant is required to check SASSA Status online. This step is essential as it prompts the system to send an SMS notification, confirming the approval and pay date for the current month. This notification confirms whether your relief funds have been approved for the specified period, allowing you to access your grant using your preferred <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/sassa-payment-methods/" data-type="link" data-id="https://sassacheck.com/sassa-payment-methods/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA payment method</a></strong>.</p><p>For those who prefer having their SASSA grant directly deposited into their bank accounts, the process is straightforward. You can easily update your banking information, ensuring that you receive your grant funds seamlessly every month, eliminating the need to visit the SAPO post office or retail outlets. On the other hand, for individuals without a bank account, alternative options are available, including utilizing services such as Pick n Pay, Boxer store, Cash Send, or the Post Office.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-when-does-sassa-r350-grant-end-or-expire">When SASSA R350 Grant End or Expire</h4><p>President Cyril Ramaphosa has reaffirmed the government’s commitment to the Social Relief of Distress (SRD) grant, recognizing its vital role in supporting the vulnerable population of more than 9 million South Africans. During his State of the Nation Address (SONA), he confirmed that R35.2 billion has been allocated to extend the SRD grant, increasing it from R350 to R370 per month per beneficiary who depends on SASSA.</p><p>Finance Minister Enoch Godongwana further emphasized this commitment, announcing that the Department of Social Development has allocated R422.3 billion for 2025 and 2026, with projections rising to R452.7 billion by 2027 and 2028. With this budget dedicated to social grant spending, SASSA continued to support millions of citizens, residents, and asylum seekers who rely on the SASSA grants to meet their basic living needs.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-how-to-check-sassa-balance">How to Check SASSA Balance</h4><p>You can check your <strong><a href="https://sassacheck.com/check-sassa-balance/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SASSA balance status</a></strong> using your bank app for online balance inquiries. This is possible for applicants who have updated their bank details for the SASSA grant. If you are using other payment options, you can dial the balance inquiry code *120*3210# to know your balance on your phone.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="htoc-sassa-payment-status-check-on-govchat">SASSA Payment Status Check on Govchat</h4><p>You can check your SASSA payment status using the GovChat platform. GovChat is an official South African government service that allows SASSA applicants to register using their cellphone numbers via the govchat.app. To check your payment status, open the app, type “SASSA” in the chat, and send “Status” to the official agent. This will provide the latest payment dates and updates on your grant.</p></div></div></article><div id="comments" class="comments-area"><h2 class="comments-title">332 Comments</h2><ol class="comment-list"><li id="comment-16829" class="comment even thread-even depth-1"><article id="div-comment-16829" class="comment-body"><footer class="comment-meta"><div class="comment-author vcard">

<a href="https://sassacheck.com/#comment-2"><time datetime=""> at </time></a></div></footer><div class="comment-content"><p>How to increase r350 grant</p></div><div class="reply"><a rel="nofollow" class="comment-reply-link" href="#comment-2" data-commentid="2" data-postid="26" data-belowelement="div-comment-2" data-respondelement="respond" data-replyto="Reply to Maria" aria-label="Reply to Maria">Reply</a></div></article><ol class="children"><li id="comment-10" class="comment byuser comment-author-social bypostauthor odd alt depth-2 parent"><article id="div-comment-10" class="comment-body"><footer class="comment-meta"><div class="comment-author vcard">
<img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSI2MCIgaGVpZ2h0PSI2MCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDYwIDYwIj48cmVjdCB3aWR0aD0iMTAwJSIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAlIiBzdHlsZT0iZmlsbDojY2ZkNGRiO2ZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eTogMC4xOyIvPjwvc3ZnPg==" alt='' data-src='https://sassacheck.com/wp-content/gravatars/852a79329634aeff85480b57a0be5463.jpg' data-srcset='https://sassacheck.com/wp-content/gravatars/15b22cefb249a5663f6944a9222fd0a5.jpg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60' loading='lazy' decoding='async'/>						<b class="fn"><a href="https://sassacheck.com" class="url" rel="ugc">Social</a></b> <span class="says">says:</span></div><div class="comment-metadata">
<a href="https://sassacheck.com/#comment-10"><time datetime=""> at </time></a></div></footer><div class="comment-content"><p>How to Increase Your R350 Grant:</p><p>To apply for an increased SASSA allowance beyond the R350 grant you currently receive, follow these steps:</p><p>1. Visit the nearest SASSA office.<br />
2. Bring these required documents:<br />
&#8211; Your 13-digit bar-coded identity document (ID).<br />
&#8211; Proof of marital status and spouse&#8217;s identity, if applicable.<br />
&#8211; A medical report or assessment report (less than three months old) indicating the need for full-time care.<br />
3. Complete the application form.<br />
4. The SASSA Officer will interview you to determine your eligibility for the grant.<br />
5. After applying, you will receive a receipt as proof of your application.</p><p>Please Note:<br />
Only you as the beneficiary or an SASSA official may fill out the form for you.</p><p>Important Notice:<br />
If you are unable to travel to the SASSA office due to age or illness, a family member or friend can apply on your behalf. They should carry a letter from you or a doctor&#8217;s note explaining the reason for your inability to visit the office.</p><p>Once approved, you will receive an increased grant of R500 per month in the form of a Grant In Aid.</p><p>Best regards,<br />
SASSACheck.com</p></div><div class="reply"><a rel="nofollow" class="comment-reply-link" href="#comment-10" data-commentid="10" data-postid="26" data-belowelement="div-comment-10" data-respondelement="respond" data-replyto="Reply to Social" aria-label="Reply to Social">Reply</a></div></article><ol class="children"><li id="comment-2407" class="comment even depth-3 parent"><article id="div-comment-2407" class="comment-body"><footer class="comment-meta"><div class="comment-author vcard">

https://sassacheck.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/fav.png 512w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></section><section id="block-9" class="widget widget_block widget_text"><p class="has-text-align-center">Dedicated to supporting individuals and families facing challenging circumstances, SASSA (South African Social Security Agency) plays a crucial role in meeting their basic needs and promoting overall well-being. By administering a diverse range of social relief grants and allowances, this organization strives to make a positive impact on the lives of South African society. Through the provision of essential financial support, SASSA effectively alleviates financial burdens, enhancing the quality of life for those in need.</p></section></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="site-bottom-footer-wrap site-footer-row-container site-footer-focus-item site-footer-row-layout-standard site-footer-row-tablet-layout-default site-footer-row-mobile-layout-default" data-section="kadence_customizer_footer_bottom"><div class="site-footer-row-container-inner"><div class="site-container"><div class="site-bottom-footer-inner-wrap site-footer-row site-footer-row-columns-1 site-footer-row-column-layout-row site-footer-row-tablet-column-layout-default site-footer-row-mobile-column-layout-row ft-ro-dir-row ft-ro-collapse-normal ft-ro-t-dir-default ft-ro-m-dir-default ft-ro-lstyle-plain"><div class="site-footer-bottom-section-1 site-footer-section footer-section-inner-items-1"><div class="footer-widget-area site-info site-footer-focus-item content-align-default content-tablet-align-default content-mobile-align-default content-valign-default content-tablet-valign-default content-mobile-valign-default" data-section="kadence_customizer_footer_html"><div class="footer-widget-area-inner site-info-inner"><div class="footer-html inner-link-style-normal"><div class="footer-html-inner"><p>This is an independent information website and is not affiliated with SASSA or the South African government.
